Let \(F(t,P)\) be the GT. Substituting the given GT constants, the GT is
\[
F(t,P)=0.8450821034\Big[(-1+P/5.1153864545)(1-P/34.4388624238)P + (1-e^{-0.0968726647352 P})P\Big].
\]
Key structural facts:

- **No \(t\)-dependence at all**. So any candidate can only match if all \(t\)-dependent parts can be eliminated by setting some candidate constants to 0 (or exponents to make terms constant, etc.).
- As a function of \(P\), GT is the sum of:
  - a **cubic polynomial** in \(P\): \(0.845\cdot P(-1+P/a)(1-P/b)\) expands to \(\alpha_1 P + \alpha_2 P^2 + \alpha_3 P^3\) with \(\alpha_3\neq 0\),
  - plus a **non-polynomial exponential term**: \(0.845\cdot P(1-e^{-kP}) = 0.845\cdot P - 0.845\cdot P e^{-kP}\), which includes the distinctive term \(P e^{-kP}\).
- Therefore any matching candidate must be able to represent **both** a nonzero \(P^3\) term **and** a term proportional to \(P e^{-kP}\) (or algebraically identical to it), while having no \(t\).

Now check candidates.

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG3)
============================================================
GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - exp(-c7*P))*P
Candidates evaluated: 101
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

**GT expression:**
```
0.845*(−1 + P/5.115)*(1 − P/34.44)*P + 0.845*(1 − exp(−0.0969*P))*P
```

Let me expand this:
- First term: `0.845*(P/5.115 − 1)*(1 − P/34.44)*P`
  - `= 0.845*(P/5.115 − P²/(5.115*34.44) − 1 + P/34.44)*P`
  - `= 0.845*(P²/5.115 − P³/(5.115*34.44) − P + P²/34.44)*`
  
Let me be more careful:
`(P/5.115 − 1)*(1 − P/34.44) = P/5.115 − P²/(5.115*34.44) − 1 + P/34.44`

Multiply by `0.845*P`:
`= 0.845*P²/5.115 − 0.845*P³/(5.115*34.44) − 0.845*P + 0.845*P²/34.44`

- Second term: `0.845*P − 0.845*P*exp(−0.0969*P)`

Combining:
`GT = −0.845*P³/(5.115*34.44) + 0.845*P²/5.115 + 0.845*P²/34.44 − 0.845*P + 0.845*P − 0.845*P*exp(−0.0969*P)`

The `−0.845*P + 0.845*P` cancels!

So: `GT = −0.845*P³/(176.1) + 0.845*P²*(1/5.115 + 1/34.44) − 0.845*P*exp(−0.0969*P)`

Computing constants:
- P³ coefficient: `−0.845/176.1 ≈ −0.004798`
- P² coefficient: `0.845*(0.1955 + 0.02904) ≈ 0.845*0.2245 ≈ 0.1897`
- Exponential term: `−0.845*P*exp(−0.0969*P)`

**GT = c_a*P³ + c_b*P² + c_c*P*exp(c_d*P)** where c_a < 0, c_d < 0.

This is a sum of: **P³, P², and P*exp(negative*P)** terms. No constant term, no P term.

Now let me check candidates for the structure: `a*P³ + b*P² + c*P*exp(d*P)` (no t-dependence, no constant).

For candidates with `t` dependence: they can only match if all `t`-dependent terms can be zeroed out.

Let me systematically check candidates that could have the right basis functions.

**Candidate 84:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3)`
This gives: P², P, P*exp(P*c3). Missing P³. Has unwanted P term (c1 can't be zero if we need to match GT which has no linear P term... wait, GT has no P term since they cancelled). So we need c1=0. But then we have P² + P*exp(P*c3), missing P³.
Candidate 84 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 85:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3 + c4)`
Same as 84 with extra constant in exponent: `P*c2*exp(c4)*exp(P*c3)` = `P*c2'*exp(P*c3)`. Same issue, missing P³.
Candidate 85 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 83:** `P³*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2/(P*c3 + 1)`
This has P³, P², and P/(P*c3+1) = rational function. The rational part `P/(Pc3+1)` cannot equal `P*exp(dP)`.
Candidate 83 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 30:** `P³*c0 + P²*c1 + P²*c2 + P*c3 + c4 + c5*log(P*c6 + 1)`
Has P³, P², P, constant, log. Missing exp. Can't match.
Candidate 30 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Let me focus on candidates with both polynomial P terms and `P*exp(P*...)` or equivalent.

**Candidate 41:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(P*c4)`
Basis: P², P, 1, exp(P*c4). GT needs P³ and P*exp(dP). Missing P³, and exp(P*c4) ≠ P*exp(dP).
Candidate 41 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 40:** `P*c0*exp(P*c1) + c2 + c3*exp(P*c4)`
Basis: P*exp(Pc1), 1, exp(Pc4). Missing P³ and P².
Candidate 40 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 38:** `P*c0*exp(P*c1) + c2 + c3*log(P*c4 + 1)`
Has P*exp(Pc1), constant, log. Missing P³, P².
Candidate 38 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 62:** `c0 + c1*exp(P*c2) + c3*exp(P*c4)`
Two exponentials plus constant. Can't produce P³ or P².
Candidate 62 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 70:** `P²*c0/(P*c1+1) + P*c2/(P*c1+1) + P*c3*exp(P*c4)`
This has a rational part `(c0*P² + c2*P)/(c1*P+1)` plus `P*c3*exp(P*c4)`.
The rational part: doing polynomial division of `c0*P² + c2*P` by `c1*P + 1`:
`= (c0/c1)*P + (c2 - c0/c1²)/(1) + ...` Actually let me be precise.

`(c0*P² + c2*P)/(c1*P + 1)` - this is a rational function. For large P it behaves as P/c1, not P³. So this can't produce a P³ term. 

Wait - but could the rational part approximate P³? No, it's degree 2/degree 1 = effectively degree 1 polynomial plus remainder. So the rational part gives effectively `aP + b + c/(c1P+1)`. Combined with `P*exp(Pc4)`, we get: aP + b + c/(c1P+1) + P*c3*exp(Pc4). This can't match P³ + P² + P*exp(dP).
Candidate 70 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 78:** `P³*c0/(P*c1+1) + P²*c2/(P*c1+1) + P²*c3/(P*c1+1) + P²*c4/(P*c1+1) + P*c5/(P*c1+1) + P*c6/(P*c1+1)`

Simplify: `[P³*c0 + P²*(c2+c3+c4) + P*(c5+c6)] / (P*c1+1)`

This is a cubic/linear rational function. Polynomial division:
`P³*c0/(c1*P+1)` = `(c0/c1)*P² - (c0/c1²)*P + (c0/c1³) - (c0/c1³)/(c1P+1)`

So overall this is a polynomial of degree 2 plus a term proportional to 1/(c1P+1). This is purely rational/polynomial - no exponential. Can't match.
Candidate 78 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 80:** Similar rational structure. No exponential.
Candidate 80 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 100:** Same type of rational function.
Candidate 100 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 53:** Same type.
Candidate 53 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Let me reconsider. The GT has the form:
`GT = a*P³ + b*P² + c*P*exp(d*P)` where d < 0.

I need candidates with P³, P², and P*exp(P*...) terms (and possibly terms that can be zeroed).

**Candidate 37:** `P*c0 + P*c1*(c2*Abs(P))**c3 + c4 + c5*exp(P*c6)`
With P ≥ 0: `P*c1*(c2*P)^c3 = c1*c2^c3 * P^(1+c3)`. If c3=2, this gives P³. Plus P, constant, exp(P*c6). Missing P² and P*exp(dP). The exp term is exp(Pc6), not P*exp(Pc6).
Candidate 37 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 35:** `P*c0*(P*c1)**c2 + P*c3 + c4 + c5*log(P*c6 + 1)`
With P ≥ 0: `c0*c1^c2 * P^(1+c2)`. If c2=2, gives P³. But has log, not exp.
Candidate 35 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2 * P^c3 * c4 + P^c2 * c5 + c6*t^c7`
= `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c4*P^(c2+c3) + c5*P^c2 + c6*t^c7`
Set c7=0 to kill t dependence (c6*1 = c6, a constant). Then we have polynomial-like terms with fractional powers. But GT needs exp(dP), which can't come from power functions.
Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 13:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c4*t^c5`
Set c5=0 → c4 is constant. Then: `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c4`
Basis: P², P, P*exp(Pc3), 1. Missing P³. Can't match.
Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Hmm, let me look for candidates that have BOTH a cubic polynomial structure AND an exponential in P.

Actually, wait. Let me reconsider candidates with `log(c*exp(P*c) + 1)` terms. The softplus function `log(exp(x)+1)` for large negative x ≈ 0, for large positive x ≈ x. But we need exact equivalence.

**Candidate 36:** `c0 + c1*exp(P*c2) + c3*log(c4*exp(P*c5) + 1)`
For this to match GT = a*P³ + b*P² + c*P*exp(dP), we'd need the combination of exp and log(exp+1) to produce P³, P², and P*exp. This seems impossible since these are fundamentally different function classes.
Candidate 36 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Similar issue.

Candidate 45 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Candidate 58 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Let me reconsider whether any candidate can produce the exact GT structure.

**Candidate 27:** `c0 + c1*exp(P*c2) + c3*Abs(P)^c4 + c5*Abs(P)^c6`

If c4=3, c6=2: `c0 + c1*exp(Pc2) + c3*P³ + c5*P²`

Hmm. Let me reconsider the GT more carefully.

GT = `−0.004798*P³ + 0.1897*P² − 0.845*P*exp(−0.0969*P)`

The key basis functions are: **P³, P², P·exp(αP)** where α < 0.

Now, `P*exp(αP)` - which candidates have this?

Candidates with `P*c*exp(P*c)`: 13, 37, 38, 40, 70, 84, 85, 87 (sin not exp)

None of these also have P³.

Wait, what about candidates where P³ can emerge from other structures?

**Candidate 94:** `P²*c0/(P*c1+1) + P*c2*(P*c3)^c4 + P*c5/(P*c1+1) + P*c6`
With P ≥ 0: The term `P*c2*(P*c3)^c4 = c2*c3^c4 * P^(1+c4)`. If c4=2, this gives `c2*c3²*P³`.
The rational part: `(c0*P² + c5*P)/(c1*P+1)` = polynomial division gives `(c0/c1)*P + (c5-c0/c1²) + (c0/c1² - c5)/(c1P+1)` approximately.
Plus P*c6.
So total: `a*P³ + b*P + c + d/(c1P+1) + e*P`
This gives P³, P, constant, 1/(c1P+1). Missing P² and P*exp(dP).
Candidate 94 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 88:** `P²*c0/(P*c1+1) + P*c2/(P*c1+1) + P^c3*c4`
Rational part + power function. If c3=3: P³ + rational(degree 1 effectively). Missing P*exp.
Candidate 88 verdict: [NO MATCH]

I'm starting to think none of these candidates match. But let me be more systematic about candidates that could potentially work.

The GT has NO t-dependence. So any candidate with t must be able to zero out all t terms.

Let me check candidates with `P*exp(P*c)` AND some way to get P³:

Looking through all candidates... I don't see any candidate that simultaneously has:
1. A P³ term (or equivalent)
2. A P² term
3. A P*exp(αP) term

Let me double-check a few more promising ones:

**Candidate 51:** `P*c0/(Pc1+c2) + P*c3*exp(Pc4)/(Pc1+c2) + c5/(Pc1+c2) + c6*exp(Pc4)/(Pc1+c2) + c7/(Pc1+c2)`

= `[P*c0 + P*c3*exp(Pc4) + c5 + c6*exp(Pc4) + c7] / (Pc1+c2)`

= `[c0*P + c3*P*exp(Pc4) + (c5+c7) + c6*exp(Pc4)] / (c1*P + c2)`

This is a ratio. For this to equal `aP³ + bP² + cP*exp(dP)`, we'd need:
`c0*P + c3*P*exp(Pc4) + K + c6*exp(Pc4) = (aP³ + bP² + cP*exp(dP))*(c1*P + c2)`

The RHS = `a*c1*P⁴ + (a*c2+b*c1)*P³ + b*c2*P² + c*c1*P²*exp(dP) + c*c2*P*exp(dP)`

The LHS has at most P*exp and P terms. The RHS has P⁴, P³, P², P²*exp, P*exp. These can't be equal.
Candidate 51 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 26:** `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + c3 + c4*exp(P*c5)`

= `P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2*[log(P(c3+c4)+c5+c6+1) - log(Pc4+1)]`
